   ābhūtis tvāṣṭro viśvarūpāt tvāṣṭrāt |	ABUtiH tvAzwraH viSva-rUpAt tvAzwrAt |
   viśvarūpas tvāṣṭro 'vśibhyām |	viSvarUpaH tvAzwraH avSiByAm |
   aśvinau dadhīca ātharvaṇāt |	aSvinO daDIcaH ATarvaNAt |
   dadhyaṅṅ ātharvaṇo 'tharvaṇo daivāt |	daDyaF ATarvaNaH aTarvaNaH dEvAt |
   atharvā daivo mṛtyoḥ prādhvaṃsanāt |	aTarvA dEvaH mRtyoH prADvaMsanAt |
   mṛtyuḥ prādhvaṃsanaḥ pradhvaṃsanāt |	mRtyuH prADvaMsanaH praDvaMsanAt |
   pradhvaṃsana ekarṣeḥ |	praDvaMsane eka-rzeH |
   ekarṣir vipracitteḥ |	eka-rziH vipracitteH |
   vipracittir vyaṣṭer |	vipracittiH vyazweH |
   vyaṣṭiḥ sanāroḥ |	vyazwiH sa-nAroH |
   sanāruḥ sanātanāt |	sanAruH sanAtanAt |
   sanātanaḥ sanagāt |	sanAtanaH sanagAt |
   sanagaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ |	sanagaH paramezWinaH |
   parameṣṭhī brahmaṇaḥ |	paramezWI brahmaNaH |
   brahma svayaṃbhu |	brahma svayaMBu |
   brahmaṇe namaḥ || BrhUp_2,6.3 ||	brahmaNe namaH || BrhUp_2,6.3 ||

   ayedānīṃ brahmavidyārthasya madhukāṇḍasya vaṃśaḥ stutyartho brahmavidyāyāḥ	ayA-idAnIm brahma-vidyA-arTasya maDu-kANxasya vaMSaH stuti-arTaH brahma-vidyAyAH
   mantraścāyaṃ svādhyāyārtho japārthaśca /	mantraH-ca-ayam svADyAya-arTaH japa-arTaH-ca /
   tatra vaṃśa iva vaṃśaḥ yathā veṇurvaṃśaḥ parvaṇaḥ parvaṇo hi bhidyate	tatra vaMSaH iva vaMSaH yaTA veNuH-vaMSaH parvaNaH parvaNaH hi Bidyate
   tadvadagratprabhṛti āmūlaprāpterayaṃ vaṃśaḥ /	tadvat-agrat-praBRti AmUla-prApteH-ayam vaMSaH /
   adhyāyacatuṣṭayasya ācāryaparamparākramo vaṃśa ityucyate /	aDyAya-catuzwayasya AcArya-paramparA-kramaH vaMSaH iti-ucyate /
   tatra prathamāntaḥ śiṣyaḥ pañcamayantaḥ ācāryaḥ /	tatra praTama-antaH SizyaH paQcamayantaH AcAryaH /
   parameṣṭhī virāṭ, brāhmaṇo hiraṇyagarbhāt /	paramezWI virAw, brAhmaNaH hiraNyagarBAt /
   tataḥ paramācāryaparamparānāsti /	tatas parama-AcArya-paramparAna-asti /
   yatpunarbrahma tannityaṃ svayambhū, tasmai brahmaṇai svayambhuve namaḥ	yat-punar-brahma tat-nityam svayamBU, tasmE brahmaNE svayamBuve namaH
   iti ṣaṣṭhaṃ brāhmaṇam //	iti zazWam brAhmaNam //
